class=\"text-muted\"><small>Published Tuesday, 05 August, 2025 at 05:51 PM</small></p>\n   224→            <div style=\"display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 10px;\">\n   225→                <img src=\"/content/images/crest-header.png\" style=\"width: 100px; height: auto;margin-bottom:15px\" />\n   226→                <div>\n   227→\n   228→\n   229→\n   230→                        <p class=\"statement-ministers text-info\" style=\"color: #31708f !important;\"><strong>Minister for Youth Justice and Victim Support and Minister for Corrective Services</strong><br />The Honourable Laura Gerber</p>\n   231→                </div>\n   232→            </div>\n   233→\n   234→\n   235→                <div class=\"pb-2 mt-4 mb-2\" style=\"margin-bottom:20px !important;text-align:center;\">\n   236→                    <h1>Crisafulli Government delivers more funding to kickstart new early intervention programs </h1>\n   237→                </div>\n   238→\n   239→            <div class=\"row\">\n   240→                <div class=\"col-md-12\">\n   241→                    <div><div>\n   242→<ul>\n   243→<li xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><strong><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"none\">Crisafulli Government is delivering a major funding boost to arrest Labor&rsquo;s Youth Crime Crisis, with&nbsp;the second round of </span><em><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"none\">Kickstarter</span></em><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"none\"> grants now open. &nbsp;</span></strong></li>\n   244→<li xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><strong><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Nearly $10 million has already gone out the door to community-led&nbsp;organisations under the first round of the $50 million </span><em><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Kickstarter</span></em><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\"> grants program.</span> </strong></li>\n   245→<li xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><strong><em><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Kickstarter</span></em><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\"> is part of a $115 million investment to deliver Gold Standard Early Intervention.</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></strong></li>\n   246→</ul>\n   247→</div>\n   248→<div>\n   249→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">The Crisafulli Government is delivering on&nbsp;a key election commitment to fund early intervention programs to break the cycle of crime, with the second round of $50 million </span><em><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Kickstarter</span></em><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\"> grants now open.</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   250→</div>\n   251→<div>\n   252→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Grants of up to $300,000 will be awarded to new Gold Standard Early Intervention programs to provide at-risk youth showing early signs of criminal behaviour,&nbsp;with the education, life skills and support to divert from a life of crime. </span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   253→</div>\n   254→<div>\n   255→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">The former Labor Government failed to properly invest in effective early intervention and rehabilitation programs, which created a generation of hardcore, repeat youth offenders. </span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   256→</div>\n   257→<div>\n   258→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">The Crisafulli Government is turning the tide on Labor&rsquo;s Youth Crime Crisis by investing $115 million to deliver Gold Standard Early Intervention programs, with $50 million to be set aside to kickstart new initiatives and $65 million to provide ongoing support to programs with proven results. &nbsp; &nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   259→</div>\n   260→<div>\n   261→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Each program will be regionally focused and tailored to meet the needs of local communities across Queensland. </span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   262→</div>\n   263→<div>\n   264→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Minister for Youth Justice and Victim Support Laura Gerber said investing in early intervention and rehabilitation was crucial to breaking the cycle of crime. </span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   265→</div>\n   266→<div>\n   267→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">&ldquo;It&rsquo;s critical we intervene early before youth go down a life of crime, and this funding allows us to support even more organisations to deliver locally led early intervention programs,&rdquo; Minister Gerber said.</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   268→</div>\n   269→<div>\n   270→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">&ldquo;For a decade, the former Labor Government failed to properly invest in early intervention, which has led to a youth crime crisis and created a generation of repeat youth offenders. </span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   271→</div>\n   272→<div>\n   273→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">&ldquo;These programs will engage youth and provide them with the support needed to go down a better path, which will help stop the cycle of crime and restore safety back to Queensland.</span></p>\n   274→</div>\n   275→<div>\n   276→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Non-government organisations, including those currently or previously delivering youth justice programs, are encouraged to consider new or expanded solutions and apply for funding.</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   277→</div>\n   278→<div>\n   279→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">For more information on the <em>Kickstarter</em> grants, including eligibility criteria and how to apply, visit <a href=\"https://linkprotect.cudasvc.com/url?a=https%3a%2f%2fyj.smartygrants.com.au%2fyjkickstarter25-26R2&amp;c=E,1,-4Yx7ChBM1NZNX_QqmkaNx2yCFuTDkWbA6PcsTOFKIT5rBJR1K87mUFr59x8-ix3x5g6Y4n9seppGuu2IM4HaGmT4MuP-8KaHdpemRnIDexJ1Wxa2IXruHfbEA,,&amp;typo=1\" aria-invalid=\"true\">https://yj.smartygrants.com.au/yjkickstarter25-26R2</a>. &nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   280→</div>\n   281→<div>\n   282→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><strong><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">ENDS</span><span          <div class=\"pb-2 mt-4 mb-2\" style=\"margin-bottom:20px !important;text-align:center;\">\n   236→                    <h1>A FRESH START FOR QUEENSLAND: Six new early intervention programs receive Kickstarter funding in Cairns to help reduce crime</h1>\n   237→                </div>\n   238→\n   239→            <div class=\"row\">\n   240→                <div class=\"col-md-12\">\n   241→                    <div><div>\n   242→<div>\n   243→<ul>\n   244→<li><strong><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">The Crisafulli Government is delivering on its commitment to provide Gold Standard Early Intervention programs to restore safety where you live.</span> </strong></li>\n   245→<li><strong><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Six new early intervention programs to help reduce crime in Cairns across the region will receive&nbsp;Kickstarter funding to deliver new programs to divert youth away from a life of crime.</span> </strong></li>\n   246→<li><strong><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\">Programs will provide community-based support, mentoring and life skill workshops for at-risk youth to help break the cycle of crime.</span> </strong></li>\n   247→<li><strong><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">After a decade of decline, the Crisafulli Government is delivering in its first 10 months to turn the tide on Labor&rsquo;s Youth Crime Crisis.</span></strong></li>\n   248→</ul>\n   249→</div>\n   250→<div>\n   251→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">The Crisafulli Government is delivering new and expanded early intervention programs to Cairns, with six community organisations receiving a share in more than $1.7 million in funding through the first round of the </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">Kickstarter</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\"> program.&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;134233117&quot;:false,&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559738&quot;:240,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   252→</div>\n   253→<div>\n   254→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">The program will provide groundbreaking early intervention programs that empower youths by providing enhanced access to educational resources, life skills development, and holistic support systems.</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;134233117&quot;:false,&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559738&quot;:240,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   255→</div>\n   256→<div>\n   257→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">Recipients include sports and activity-based learning, mentorship programs, life skill workshops and culturally led activities tailored towards First Nations young people.&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;134233117&quot;:false,&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559738&quot;:240,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   258→</div>\n   259→<div>\n   260→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">A decade of failure by the former Labor Government saw inadequate investment in effective early intervention measures and weak laws, which created a generation of serious repeat offenders, creating Labor's Youth Crime Crisis.&nbsp; </span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;134233117&quot;:false,&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559738&quot;:240,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   261→</div>\n   262→<div>\n   263→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">The $50 million Kickstarter program is a key component of the Crisafulli Government&rsquo;s $115 million strategy to deliver Gold Standard Early Intervention across the state and restore safety where you live.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;134233117&quot;:false,&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559738&quot;:240,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   264→</div>\n   265→<div>\n   266→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">The community organisations receiving funding include:</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;134233117&quot;:false,&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559738&quot;:240,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   267→</div>\n   268→<div>\n   269→<ul trauma-informed, psychoeducational initiative designed to support parents and caregivers of at-risk children and youth aged 8&ndash;17 who are vulnerable to involvement with the Youth Justice system. It provides evidence-based tools to enhance emotional regulation, reduce family conflict, and strengthen relationships. The program combines workshops, personalised counselling, and assessments with culturally responsive approaches to strengthen families, build resilience, and create safer more connected homes. </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"none\"> </span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559739&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   305→</div>\n   306→<div>\n   307→<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">ACCER Care PL &ndash; YD Project</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\"> &ndash; Bridgeman Downs</span></span></p>\n   308→</div>\n   309→<div>\n   310→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">The YD Project is a 12-week early intervention initiative aimed at empowering Indigenous youth aged 8&ndash;17 years through individualised case management, mentoring, and cultural activities aimed at fostering positive life choices. The program emphasises early intervention and community-led solutions, with an optional extended 12-week phase for participants requiring additional support to achieve their goals. </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"none\"> </span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559739&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   311→</div>\n   312→<div>\n   313→<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Inspiring Brighter Futures Foundation &ndash; Onwards &amp; Upwards Wellbeing Mentoring program </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">&ndash; Wynnum West</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\"> </span></span></p>\n   314→</div>\n   315→<div>\n   316→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">The Onwards &amp; Upwards Wellbeing Mentoring program is a 12-month initiative supporting at-risk youth aged 12 to 17, with a focus on Indigenous participants, through personalised mentoring, run coaching, and education in well-being, leadership, and vocational skills. Co-designed with Indigenous communities, the program aims to reduce recidivism, improve mental health, and empower young people to achieve positive, purpose-driven futures, transitioning them into ongoing community support groups. </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"none\"> </span>&nbsp;<br><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\"> </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\"> </span>&nbsp;<br><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Queensland Blue Light Association Inc &ndash; Blue Edge </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">&ndash; Aspley</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\"> </span></span></p>\n   317→</div>\n   318→<div>\n   319→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Blue Edge is an eight-week program supporting at-risk young people by enhancing mental and physical wellbeing, building leadership and resilience, and reducing low-level crime through positive behaviours and community connections. Delivered twice weekly, it combines physical training, life skills workshops, and peer-led mentorship, fostering trust, personal growth, and respectful relationships with police, culminating in a celebratory graduation event. </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"none\"> </span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559739&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   320→</div>\n   321→<div>\n   322→<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Kirrawe Indigenous Corporation &ndash; Walama Ngurra Bangaba: Returning home building futures </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">- Loganholme</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\"> </span></span></p>\n   323→</div>\n   324→<div>\n   325→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Walama Ngurra Bangaba is a 12-month trauma-informed program for First Nations youth aged 8&ndash;17, focusing on re-engaging them with education, training, or employment while strengthening cultural and community connections. Through tailored, hands-on learning and holistic support, the program aims to reduce youth crime, improve educational outcomes, and foster safer, stronger communities. </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"none\"> </span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559739&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   326→</div>\n   327→<div>\n   328→<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Royal Society for the Prevention of Cruelty to Animals Ltd &ndash; Tails of Change </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">- Wacol</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\"> </span></span></p>\n   329→</div>\n   330→<div>\n   331→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Tails of Change is a two-year early intervention program using hands-on animal care to help disengaged youth aged 11-17 build empathy, emotional regulation, and pro-social behaviours, reducing the risk of offending. By fostering responsibility and accountability, the program addresses underlying issues such as trauma and neglect, promoting emotional development and preventing future harm. </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"none\"> </span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559739&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   332→</div>\n   333→<div>\n   334→<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Youth Retreat Centre &ndash; Reconnect with Culture and Community </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">- Ipswich</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\"> </span></span></p>\n   335→</div>\n   336→<div>\n   337→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Reconnect with Culture and Community is a 12-month outreach program in Ipswich offering intensive case management, mentoring, and tailored referrals to support First Nations and general youth ages 14-17. Through cultural reconnection, life skills development, and pathways to education and employment, the initiative addresses risk factors linked to offending while fostering belonging, self-worth, and positive community engagement. </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"none\"> </span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559739&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   338→</div>\n   339→<div>\n   340→<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">V.I.T.A.L. Projex &ndash; STRONG Futures (Strength, Trust, Respect, Opportunity, New Ground)</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\"> </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">- Ipswich</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\"> </span></span></p>\n   341→</div>\n   342→<div>\n   343→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">STRONG Futures is a 12-month, trauma-informed early intervention program for 80 young people aged 10&ndash;17 in Ipswich, combining culturally safe mentoring, technology-assisted emotional regulation, and skills training to reduce anti-social behaviour and reoffending. Delivered in four 10-week cohorts, the program includes adventure-based therapy, VR-based self-reflection, neurofeedback brain training, and culturally co-designed support to foster resilience, education, and community reintegration. </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"none\"> </span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559739&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   344→</div>\n   345→<div>\n   346→<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Dynamic Community Care Pty Ltd &ndash; The Durungal Program </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">- Ipswich</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\"> </span></span></p>\n   347→</div>\n   348→<div>\n   349→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">The Durungal program is an eight-week intervention for youths aged 10-17, focusing on non-violent conflict resolution, aggression reduction, and social skill development through weekly or fortnightly face-to-face sessions. Delivered by a qualified facilitator in a confidential setting, the program includes tailored learning plans, case notes, and practical exercises, with flexible locations such as schools, homes, or community centres. </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"none\"> </span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559739&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   350→</div>\n   351→<div>\n   352→<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Gunya Meta &ndash; Strong Warriors Strong Future </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">&ndash; Logan Central</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\"> </span></span></p>\n   353→</div>\n   354→<div>\n   355→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Strong Warriors Strong Future is an 18-month, culturally-led program for 20 First Nations young people aged 10&ndash;17 in Logan, delivered by Gunya Meta to strengthen cultural identity, kinship, and family inclusion. Through Kinship Mentors, cultural immersion, and trauma-informed workshops, the program fosters emotional regulation, healthy relationships, and pro-social pathways to reduce early criminal behaviours and empower youth and families. </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"none\"> </span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559739&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   356→</div>\n   357→<div>\n   358→<p><span style=\"text-decoration: underline;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Legacy Connect (Cultural Wellbeing Services) - Legacy Cultural Youth Program</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\"> </span><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">&ndash; Springfield Lakes</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\"> </span></span></p>\n   359→</div>\n   360→<div>\n   361→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">The Legacy Cultural Youth Program (LCYP) is a two-year, trauma-informed initiative supporting at-risk Pasifika, CALD, and Indigenous youth aged 10&ndash;17 in Ipswich and West Moreton through culturally grounded workshops and one-on-one mentoring. By addressing disengagement, trauma, and complex needs, the program aims to improve emotional regulation, school attendance, cultural pride, and reduce anti-social behaviour, fostering stronger, healthier communities.</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"none\"> </span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559739&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   362→</div></div>\n   363→                </div>\n   364→            </div>\n          <div class=\"pb-2 mt-4 mb-2\" style=\"margin-bottom:20px !important;text-align:center;\">\n   238→                    <h1>Three new early intervention programs to help make Toowoomba safer </h1>\n   239→                </div>\n   240→\n   241→            <div class=\"row\">\n   242→                <div class=\"col-md-12\">\n   243→                    <div><div>\n   244→<div>\n   245→<ul>\n   246→<li xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><strong><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"none\">Crisafulli Government is delivering on a key election commitment for community-led early intervention programs for the Toowoomba region. </span> </strong></li>\n   247→<li xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><strong><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"none\">Three new Kickstarter early intervention programs will be delivered to help make Toowoomba safer.</span> </strong></li>\n   248→<li xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><strong><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"none\">Programs are part of a $115 million investment to deliver Gold Standard Early Intervention in the&nbsp;Crisafulli Government&rsquo;s Making Our Community Safer Plan.&nbsp;</span></strong></li>\n   249→<li xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><strong><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"none\">The Government is delivering safety where you live, and a fresh start for Queensland.</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;134233117&quot;:false,&quot;134233118&quot;:false,&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559738&quot;:240,&quot;335559739&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:252}\">&nbsp;</span></strong></li>\n   250→</ul>\n   251→</div>\n   252→<div>\n   253→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">The Crisafulli Government is delivering on its election commitment with three new community-led youth early intervention programs in the Toowoomba region to help restore safety where you live. </span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;134233117&quot;:false,&quot;134233118&quot;:false,&quot;335551550&quot;:0,&quot;335551620&quot;:0,&quot;335559738&quot;:240,&quot;335559739&quot;:220}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   254→</div>\n   255→<div>\n   256→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">The programs will be delivered with Kickstarter funding as part of the Crisafulli Government&rsquo;s $115 million investment in Gold Standard Early Intervention across Queensland to prevent crime before it starts and reduce victims of crime.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;134233117&quot;:false,&quot;134233118&quot;:false,&quot;335551550&quot;:0,&quot;335551620&quot;:0,&quot;335559738&quot;:240,&quot;335559739&quot;:220}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   257→</div>\n   258→<div>\n   259→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">The three new programs for the Toowoomba region are:</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;134233117&quot;:false,&quot;134233118&quot;:false,&quot;335551550&quot;:0,&quot;335551620&quot;:0,&quot;335559738&quot;:240,&quot;335559739&quot;:220}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   260→</div>\n   261→<div>\n   262→<ul style=\"list-style-type: disc;\" role=\"list\">\n   263→<li role=\"listitem\" data-aria-level=\"1\" data-aria-posinset=\"1\" data-list-defn-props=\"{&quot;335552541&quot;:1,&quot;335559683&quot;:0,&quot;335559684&quot;:-2,&quot;335559685&quot;:720,&quot;335559991&quot;:360,&quot;469769226&quot;:&quot;Symbol&quot;,&quot;469769242&quot;:[8226],&quot;469777803&quot;:&quot;left&quot;,&quot;469777804&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;469777815&quot;:&quot;hybridMultilevel&quot;}\" data-listid=\"30\" data-font=\"Symbol\" data-leveltext=\"\" aria-setsize=\"-1\">\n   264→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">Adapt Mentorship Indigenous Corporation 12-month program will deliver culturally responsive mentoring, creative activities and tailored support to reduce crime and promote positive behaviour for First Nations youth aged 8-17.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;134233117&quot;:false,&quot;134233118&quot;:false,&quot;335551550&quot;:0,&quot;335551620&quot;:0,&quot;335559738&quot;:240,&quot;335559739&quot;:0}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   265→</li>\n   266→</ul>\n   267→</div>\n   268→<div>\n   269→<ul style=\"list-style-type: disc;\" role=\"list\">\n   270→<li role=\"listitem\" data-aria-level=\"1\" data-aria-posinset=\"2\" data-list-defn-props=\"{&quot;335552541&quot;:1,&quot;335559683&quot;:0,&quot;335559684&quot;:-2,&quot;335559685&quot;:720,&quot;335559991&quot;:360,&quot;469769226&quot;:&quot;Symbol&quot;,&quot;469769242&quot;:[8226],&quot;469777803&quot;:&quot;left&quot;,&quot;469777804&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;469777815&quot;:&quot;hybridMultilevel&quot;}\" data-listid=\"30\" data-font=\"Symbol\" data-leveltext=\"\" aria-setsize=\"-1\">\n   271→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">Downs Industry Schools Co-operation Inc Step Up Now program 5-month program will support at-risk youth to develop life skills, resilience, and to transition into education, employment, or training.&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;134233117&quot;:false,&quot;134233118&quot;:false,&quot;335551550&quot;:0,&quot;335551620&quot;:0,&quot;335559738&quot;:240,&quot;335559739&quot;:0}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   272→</li>\n   273→</ul>\n   274→</div>\n   275→<div>\n   276→<ul style=\"list-style-type: disc;\" role=\"list\">\n   277→<li role=\"listitem\" data-aria-level=\"1\" data-aria-posinset=\"3\" data-list-defn-props=\"{&quot;335552541&quot;:1,&quot;335559683&quot;:0,&quot;335559684&quot;:-2,&quot;335559685&quot;:720,&quot;335559991&quot;:360,&quot;469769226&quot;:&quot;Symbol&quot;,&quot;469769242&quot;:[8226],&quot;469777803&quot;:&quot;left&quot;,&quot;469777804&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;469777815&quot;:&quot;hybridMultilevel&quot;}\" data-listid=\"30\" data-font=\"Symbol\" data-leveltext=\"\" aria-setsize=\"-1\">\n   278→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">Village Support Limited&rsquo;s Where We All Belong initiative will support young people and their families, working in partnership with schools to deliver tailored supports, combining, sports, cultural programs, career workshops and family forums to reduce offending behaviour.&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;134233117&quot;:false,&quot;134233118&quot;:false,&quot;335551550&quot;:0,&quot;335551620&quot;:0,&quot;335559738&quot;:240,&quot;335559739&quot;:0}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   279→</li>\n   280→</ul>\n   281→</div>\n   282→<div>\n   283→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">For a decade, Labor&rsquo;s weak laws, fewer police and lack of early intervention created a generation of serious repeat offenders.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;134233117&quot;:false,&quot;134233118&quot;:false,&quot;335551550&quot;:0,&quot;335551620&quot;:0,&quot;335559738&quot;:240,&quot;335559739&quot;:220}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   284→</div>\n   285→<div>\n   286→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">Premier David Crisafulli said the Government was delivering the fresh start Queenslanders voted data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;134233117&quot;:false,&quot;134233118&quot;:false,&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335551550&quot;:0,&quot;335551620&quot;:0,&quot;335559738&quot;:240,&quot;335559739&quot;:240,&quot;335559740&quot;:276}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   287→</div>\n   288→<div>\n   289→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">&ldquo;We are helping make Queensland safer with more police, stronger laws, early intervention and rehabilitation,&rdquo; Premier Crisafulli said.</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;134233117&quot;:false,&quot;134233118&quot;:false,&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335551550&quot;:0,&quot;335551620&quot;:0,&quot;335559738&quot;:240,&quot;335559739&quot;:240,&quot;335559740&quot;:276}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   293→</div>\n   294→<div>\n   295→<p xml:lang=\"EN-US\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">&ldquo;Only with Adult Crime, Adult Time, more police, rehabilitation and early intervention align-items: center; gap: 10px;\">\n   225→                <img src=\"/content/images/crest-header.png\" style=\"width: 100px; height: auto;margin-bottom:15px\" />\n   226→                <div>\n   227→\n   228→\n   229→\n   230→                        <p class=\"statement-ministers text-info\" style=\"color: #31708f !important;\"><strong>Minister for Youth Justice and Victim Support and Minister for Corrective Services</strong><br />The Honourable Laura Gerber</p>\n   231→                </div>\n   232→            </div>\n   233→\n   234→\n   235→                <div class=\"pb-2 mt-4 mb-2\" style=\"margin-bottom:20px !important;text-align:center;\">\n   236→                    <h1>Three new early intervention programs to help make Central Queensland &amp; Wide Bay safer </h1>\n   237→                </div>\n   238→\n   239→            <div class=\"row\">\n   240→                <div class=\"col-md-12\">\n   241→                    <div><div>\n   242→<div>\n   243→<ul>\n   244→<li><strong><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Crisafulli Government i</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">s delivering three new Gold Standard Early Intervention programs for Central Queensland and the Wide Bay, to help restore safety where you live.</span></span></strong></li>\n   245→<li><strong><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Program will provide cultural mentoring, employment readiness courses, and skills development training for at-risk youth.</span></span></strong></li>\n   246→<li><strong><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">The&nbsp;Crisafulli Government is investing $115 million to deliver Gold Standard Early Intervention, to turn the tide on Labor&rsquo;s Youth Crime Crisis and make Queensland safer.</span></span></strong></li>\n   247→<li><strong><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\">The&nbsp;Crisafulli Government is delivering safety where you live and a fresh start for Queensland.</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></span></strong></li>\n   248→</ul>\n   249→</div>\n   250→<div>\n   251→<p><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">The Crisafulli Government is delivering on its election commitment to restore safety where you live with three new early intervention programs for Central Queensland and the Wide Bay.</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></span></p>\n   252→</div>\n   253→<div>\n   254→<p><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">It is one of the ways the Crisafulli Government is delivering a fresh start for Queensland after crime skyrocketed during the former Labor Government&rsquo;s decade of decline.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></span></p>\n   255→</div>\n   256→<div>\n   257→<p><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Central Queensland Indigenous Development will receive almost $900,000 to deliver the new programs in Rockhampton, Woorabinda and Bundaberg for at-risk youth aged 13&ndash;17.</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></span></p>\n   258→</div>\n   259→<div>\n   260→<p><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Participants will undertake a 12-week employment readiness course, cultural mentorship, and skills development activities to promote positive behaviour and a pathway to education, training or employment.</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></span></p>\n   261→</div>\n   262→<div>\n   263→<p><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">The programs will be delivered with Kickstarter funding as part of the Crisafulli Government&rsquo;s $115 million investment in Gold Standard Early Intervention, helping make Queensland safer by intervening early with youth, become they become entrenched in a life of crime.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></span></p>\n   264→</div>\n   265→<div>\n   266→<p><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">Labor&rsquo;s weak laws, fewer police, and failure to invest in early intervention created a generation of serious repeat youth offenders and the Queensland Youth Crime Crisis.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></span></p>\n   267→</div>\n   268→<div>\n   269→<p><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">The Crisafulli Government is restoring safety where you live with stronger laws, more police, and the biggest investment in rehabilitation and early intervention in Queensland history.&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></span></p>\n   270→</div>\n   271→<div>\n   272→<p><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Minister for Youth Justice and Victim Support Laura Gerber said the Crisafulli Government was delivering the fresh start Queenslanders voted for, exactly as promised.&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></span></p>\n   273→</div>\n   274→<div>\n   275→<p><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">&ldquo;We are delivering safety where you live by investing in early intervention programs in Central Queensland and the Wide Bay to break Labor&rsquo;s cycle of crime,&rdquo; Minister Gerber said.</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></span></p>\n   276→</div>\n   277→<div>\n   278→<p><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">&ldquo;Labor&rsquo;s failure to properly fund effective early intervention programs led to a decade of increasing numbers of youth offenders and victims of crime.  &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></span></p>\n   279→</div>\n   280→<div>\n   281→<p><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">&ldquo;The Crisafulli Government is investing in early intervention programs to help at-risk youth build a better future and to steer them away from a life of crime while providing the support needed to re-engage with the community, education or employment.&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></span></p>\n   282→</div>\n   283→<div>\n   284→<p><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"none\">&ldquo;While we are seeing crime down and victim numbers down, there is much more to be done to make Queensland safer, and we remain committed to delivering the fresh start we promised.&rdquo;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></span></p>\n   285→</div>\n   286→</div>\n   287→<div>\n   288→<p><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">\"The Crisafulli Government is committed to making Queensland safer and early intervention is crucial to preventing the next generation of youth offenders,&rdquo; Mrs Kirkland said.</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></span></p>\n   292→</div>\n   293→<div>\n   294→<p><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; Mr Dillon said.</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></span></p>\n   298→</div>\n   299→<div>\n   300→<p><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; Mr Bennett said.&nbsp;</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"auto\">&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;201341983&quot;:0,&quot;335559740&quot;:240}\">&nbsp;</span></span></p>\n   310→</div>\n   311→<div>\n   312→<p><span style=\"font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif;        <div><div>\n   242→<div>\n   243→<ul>\n   244→<li><strong><span xml:lang=\"EN-AU\" data-contrast=\"none\">Crisafulli Government is delivering a new early intervention program   248→</ul>\n   249→</div>\n   250→<div>\n   251→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\">The Crisafulli Government is breaking the cycle of crime and restoring safety where you live with a data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;335559739&quot;:120,&quot;335559746&quot;:50}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   252→</div>\n   253→<div>\n   254→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\">It is just one way the Crisafulli Government is making Queensland safer after crime skyrocketed during Labor&rsquo;s decade of decline.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;335559739&quot;:120,&quot;335559746&quot;:50}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   255→</div>\n   256→<div>\n   257→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\">Fresh Start Academy will support at-risk youth aged 10 to 17 years old across Townsville with their hands-on Kickstarter&nbsp;barbering&nbsp;program that puts youth on a path away from crime and towards education,&nbsp;training&nbsp;or a job.</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   258→</div>\n   259→<div>\n   260→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\">Participants will undertake a 20-week&nbsp;program that provides&nbsp;tailored&nbsp;mentoring,&nbsp;educational&nbsp;workshops&nbsp;and&nbsp;accredited&nbsp;training,&nbsp;including barbering, first aid,&nbsp;RSA&nbsp;and&nbsp;barista courses.&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   261→</div>\n   262→<div>\n   263→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\">The program is funded under the Crisafulli Government&rsquo;s&nbsp;</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\">Kickstarter&nbsp;</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\">early intervention grants and helps make Townsville safer by intervening early before youth become entrenched in a life of crime.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   264→</div>\n   265→<div>\n   266→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\">Kickstarter&nbsp;</span><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\">funds early intervention programs for at-risk youth showing early signs of criminal&nbsp;behaviour&nbsp;to re-engage them with education,&nbsp;employment&nbsp;and the community.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;335559739&quot;:120,&quot;335559746&quot;:50}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   267→</div>\n   268→<div>\n   269→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\">Labor&rsquo;s weak laws, fewer&nbsp;police&nbsp;and failure to invest in early intervention created a generation of serious repeat youth offenders and Queensland&rsquo;s Youth Crime Crisis.&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;335559739&quot;:120,&quot;335559746&quot;:50}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   270→</div>\n   271→<div>\n   272→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\">The Crisafulli Queensland&rsquo;s&nbsp;history.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{&quot;335559739&quot;:120,&quot;335559746&quot;:50}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   273→</div>\n   274→<div>\n   275→<p><span future.</span><span data-ccp-props=\"{}\">&nbsp;</span></p>\n   288→</div>\n   289→<div>\n   290→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\">&ldquo;This program uses&nbsp;education and training 296→<div>\n   297→<p><span xml:lang=\"EN-US\" data-contrast=\"auto\">&ldquo;Our&nbsp;community suffered&nbsp;during Labor&rsquo;s Youth Crime Crisis and early-intervention programs, like this PM</small></p>\n   224→            <div style=\"display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 10px;\">\n   225→                <img src=\"/content/images/crest-header.png\" style=\"width: 100px; height: auto;margin-bottom:15px\" />\n   226→                <div>\n   227→\n   228→\n   229→\n   230→                        <p class=\"statement-ministers text-info\" style=\"color: #31708f !important;\"><strong>Minister for Youth Justice and Victim Support and Minister for Corrective Services</strong><br />The Honourable Laura Gerber</p>\n   231→                </div>\n   232→            </div>\n   233→\n   234→\n   235→                <div class=\"pb-2 mt-4 mb-2\" style=\"margin-bottom:20px !important;text-align:center;\">\n   236→                    <h1>Kickstarting early intervention to make Brisbane safer</h1>\n   237→                </div>\n   238→\n   239→            <div class=\"row\">\n   240→                <div class=\"col-md-12\">\n   241→                    <div><ul>\n   242→<li><strong>The Crisafulli Government is delivering four new early intervention programs across Greater Brisbane to restore safety where you live.</strong></li>\n   243→<li><strong>Programs provide education, mentoring, and life-skills workshops to divert at-risk youth away from crime.</strong></li>\n   244→<li><strong>The Crisafulli Government is delivering Gold Standard Early Intervention to stop crime before it starts and make Queensland safer.</strong></li>\n   245→<li><strong>The Crisafulli Government's stronger laws, more police, early intervention and rehabilitation is starting to turn the tide on Labor&rsquo;s Youth Crime Crisis, delivering a 7.2 per cent drop in the number of victims of crime in 2025.</strong></li>\n   246→</ul>\n   247→<p>The Crisafulli Government is breaking the cycle of crime and restoring safety where you live with four new Kickstarter early intervention programs across the Greater Brisbane region.</p>\n   248→<p>It is just one way the Crisafulli Government is delivering for the region and making Queensland safer after crime skyrocketed during Labor&rsquo;s decade of decline.&nbsp;</p>\n   249→<p>The four programs support at-risk youth across Brisbane City, Moreton Bay and Redlands to re-engage them with education, training and their community.</p>\n   250→<p>The programs are funded under the Crisafulli Government&rsquo;s Kickstarter early intervention grants and help make the region safer by intervening early before youth become entrenched in a life of crime.</p>\n   251→<p>Traction for Young People, Music Beat Australia, Deception Bay Neighbourhood&nbsp; Centre and Inspire Youth and Family Services shared in more than $1 million funding under the Crisafulli Government&rsquo;s Kickstarter grants.</p>\n   252→<p>Labor&rsquo;s weak laws, fewer police and failure to invest in early intervention created a generation of serious repeat youth offenders and Queensland&rsquo;s Youth Crime Crisis.</p>\n   253→<p>The Crisafulli Government is restoring safety where you live with stronger laws, more police, and the biggest investment in rehabilitation and early intervention in Queensland history.</p>\n   254→<p>Minister for Youth Justice and Victim Support Laura Gerber said the Crisafulli Government was delivering new, community-led early intervention programs right across the state to make Queensland safer.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>\n   255→<p>&ldquo;We introduced our tough Adult Crime, Adult Time laws to hold offenders to account but, we are also investing in early intervention because it&rsquo;s a critical step to stop youth from falling into a life of crime,&rdquo; Minister Gerber said.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>\n   256→<p>&ldquo;Addressing the early signs of disengagement, anti-social or criminal behaviour is critical to breaking the cycle of crime and putting youth back on the right track.</p>\n   257→<p>&ldquo;We are delivering safety where you live with tough laws, more police, early intervention, and rehabilitation to break Labor&rsquo;s cycle of crime for good.&rdquo;</p>\n   258→<p><strong>ENDS</strong></p>\n   259→<p><strong>MEDIA CONTACT: </strong>Ashley Pillhofer &ndash; 0450 619 603</p>\n   260→<p><strong>ADDITIONAL INFORMATION:&nbsp;</strong></p>\n   261→<p><strong>Traction for Young People &ndash; The NextGEN BUILD Redlands program </strong></p>\n   262→<p>The NextGEN BUILD Redlands program combines bike-building alongside mentoring to support at-risk youth aged 10&ndash;15. The program is delivered over a 9-week school term with a focus on school engagement and community reintegration to reduce long-term offending risks.</p>\n   263→<p><strong>Music Beat Australia &ndash; Changing the Tune</strong></p>\n   264→<p>Changing the Tune is a 14-month music therapy project for at-risk, neurodivergent youth in Brisbane aimed at improving emotional regulation to reduce criminal behaviour. Delivered through group drumming, songwriting, jam sessions, and individual support, the program fosters emotional literacy, social connectedness, and pro-social engagement.</p>\n   265→<p><strong>Deception Bay Neighbourhood Centre &ndash; STEP-UP: Early Intervention for Children 8&ndash;12 Developing Accountability and Emotional Regulation in Deception Bay</strong></p>\n   266→<p>A 12-week early intervention program in Deception Bay for youth aged 8-12 who are showing early signs of antisocial behaviour and social disengagement. Alongside group mentoring sessions, the program also works with young people&rsquo;s families to build stronger family and school connections. &nbsp;</p>\n   267→<p><strong>Inspire Youth and Family Services &ndash; Inspire Positive Redirection Program</strong></p>\n   268→<p>A community-led early intervention program in Inala for youth aged 8&ndash;17 who are engaging in antisocial or early criminal behaviour. Combining mentoring, family support, and community engagement, the program helps to redirect participants onto positive life pathways.</p></div>\n   269→                </div>\n   270→            </div>\n   271→\n   272→            <div class=\"statement-attachments\">\n   273→            </div>\n   274→        </div>\n   275→    </div>\n   276→</div>\n   277→                    <div <div>\n   223→            <p class=\"text-muted\"><small>Published Thursday, 26 February, 2026 at 11:00 AM</small></p>\n   224→            <div style=\"display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 10px;\">\n   225→                <img src=\"/content/images/crest-header.png\" style=\"width: 100px; height: auto;margin-bottom:15px\" />\n   226→                <div>\n   227→\n   228→\n   229→\n   230→                        <p class=\"statement-ministers text-info\" style=\"color: #31708f !important;\"><strong>Minister for Youth Justice and Victim Support and Minister for Corrective Services</strong><br />The Honourable Laura Gerber</p>\n   231→                </div>\n   232→            </div>\n   233→\n   234→\n   235→                <div class=\"pb-2 mt-4 mb-2\" style=\"margin-bottom:20px !important;text-align:center;\">\n   236→                    <h1>Kickstarting early intervention to keep youth out of crime</h1>\n   237→                </div>\n   238→\n   239→            <div class=\"row\">\n   240→                <div class=\"col-md-12\">\n   241→                    <div><ul>\n   242→<li><strong>Crisafulli Government is delivering two new early intervention programs for Ipswich and Logan to restore safety where you live. </strong></li>\n   243→<li><strong>Programs will provide vocational training, education, mentoring, and community engagement to divert at-risk youth away from crime. </strong></li>\n   244→<li><strong>The Crisafulli Government is investing $115 million to stop crime before it starts with Gold Standard Early Intervention.</strong></li>\n   245→<li><strong>Stronger laws, more police, early intervention and rehabilitation is starting to turn the tide on Labor&rsquo;s Youth Crime Crisis, delivering a 7.2 per cent drop in the number of victims of crime in 2025.</strong></li>\n   246→</ul>\n   247→<p>The Crisafulli Government is breaking the cycle of crime and restoring safety where you live with two new<em> Kickstarter </em>early intervention programs in Logan and Ipswich.</p>\n   248→<p>It is just one way the Crisafulli Government is making Queensland safer after crime skyrocketed during Labor&rsquo;s decade of decline.</p>\n   249→<p>The BUSY Group will support at-risk girls aged 14&ndash;17 across Logan with their 10-week <em>Kickstarter</em> program that provides mentoring and teaches girls trade skills to turn their lives away from crime and reconnect them with education, training, or a job.</p>\n   250→<p>Sudanese-Australian Lost Boys and Girls of South Sudan support at-risk youth aged 8-17 with intensive mentoring, family engagement, skill-building and cultural support to re-engage them with education and the community.</p>\n   251→<p>The programs are funded under the Crisafulli Government&rsquo;s <em>Kickstarter</em> early intervention grants and helps make Logan and Ipswich safer by intervening early before youth become entrenched in a life of crime.</p>\n   252→<p>Labor&rsquo;s weak laws, fewer police and failure to invest in early intervention created a generation of serious repeat youth offenders and Queensland&rsquo;s Youth Crime Crisis.</p>\n   253→<p>The Crisafulli Government is restoring safety where you live with stronger laws, more police, and the biggest investment in rehabilitation and early intervention in Queensland history.</p>\n   254→<p>Minister for Youth Justice and Victim Support Laura Gerber said early intervention was vital to making Queensland safer and reducing victims of crime.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>\n   255→<p>&ldquo;We are investing in early intervention because we know it&rsquo;s a critical step to prevent youth from falling into a life of crime,&rdquo; Minister Gerber said.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>\n   256→<p>&ldquo;Addressing the early signs of disengagement, anti-social or criminal behaviour is critical to breaking the cycle of crime and putting youth back on the right track.&rdquo;&nbsp;</p>\n   257→<p>The BUSY Group General Manager of Youth and Community Glen O&rsquo;Keefe said early, tailored support could change the direction of a young person&rsquo;s life.</p>\n   258→<p>&ldquo;When young people disengage early, the impacts can follow them for years,&rdquo; Mr O&rsquo;Keefe said.</p>\n   259→<p>&ldquo;This program is about restoring self-belief, building aspirations, and helping young women connect to education, training and employment in a way that makes sense for them.&rdquo;&nbsp;</p>\n   260→<p>Sudanese-Australian Lost Boys and Girls of South Sudan Treasurer Gabriel Pioth said Kickstarter funding was an investment in the future of youth. &nbsp;</p>\n   261→<p>&ldquo;By creating safe spaces and trusted relationships, we can help prevent disengagement and reduce the risk of young people heading down harmful or unsafe pathways,&rdquo; Mr Pioth said.</p>\n   262→<p>&ldquo;This funding represents a significant investment in the future of young people in our community and it enables us to provide structured trauma informed support, mentoring and practical pathways that guide young people toward education, training and employment.&rdquo;</p>\n   263→<p><strong>ENDS</strong></p>\n   264→<p><strong>MEDIA CONTACT:</strong> Ashley Pillhofer 0450 619 603</p></div>\n   265→                </div>\n   266→            </div>\n   267→\n   268→                  <div class=\"qld__accordion__body-wrapper\">\n  1004→                                <p><strong>Adapt Mentorship Indigenous Corporation </strong></p><p>Project: Adapt Youth Mentorship Program</p><p>This 12-month program will deliver culturally responsive mentoring, creative activities, and tailored support to reduce crime and promote positive behaviour for First Nations youth aged 8-17.</p><p>Location: Toowoomba</p><p><strong>Downs Industry Schools Co-operation Incorporate</strong></p><p>Project: Step Up Now (SUN)</p><p>SUN is a 5-month program that will support at-risk youth to develop life skills, resilience, and to transition into education, employment, or training.</p><p>Location: Toowoomba</p><p><strong>Dynamic Community Care Pty Ltd </strong></p><p>Project: The Durungal Program</p><p>An eight-week intervention for youths aged 10&ndash;17 years, focusing on non-violent conflict resolution, aggression reduction, and social skills development through weekly or fortnightly face-to-face sessions delivered by a qualified facilitator in a confidential setting.</p><p>Location: Ipswich and Toowoomba</p><p><strong>Legacy Connect (Cultural Wellbeing Services)</strong></p><p>Project: Legacy Cultural Youth Program (Springfield Lakes)</p><p>This two-year, trauma-informed initiative supports at-risk Pasifika, culturally and linguistically diverse (CALD), and Indigenous youths aged 10&ndash;17 years in Ipswich and West Moreton through culturally grounded workshops and one-on-one mentoring.</p><p>Location: Ipswich</p><p><strong>Village Support Limited </strong></p><p>Project: Where We All Belong</p><p>This program will support youth and their families, working in partnership with schools to deliver tailored supports, combining sports, cultural programs, career workshops, and family forums to reduce offending behaviour.</p><p>Location: Toowoomba</p><p><strong>V.I.T.A.L. Projex</strong></p><p>Project: STRONG Futures (Strength, Trust, Respect, Opportunity, New Ground)</p><p>STRONG Futures is a 12-month, trauma-informed early intervention program delivered in four 10-week cohorts to provide youths aged 10&ndash;17 years the opportunity to improve anti-social behaviour and reduce reoffending.</p><p>Location: Ipswich</p><p><strong>Youth Retreat Centre </strong></p><p>Project: Reconnect with Culture and Community</p><p>An outreach program in Ipswich offering intensive case management over 12-months, including mentoring, and tailored referrals to support First Nations and general youth aged 14&ndash;17 years.</p><p>Location: Ipswich</p>\n  1005→                            </div>\n  1006→                        </div>\n  1007→                    </section>\n  1008→                </li>\n  1009→                <li>\n  1010→                    <section class=\"qld__accordion\">\n  1011→                        <button class=\"qld__accordion__title js-qld__accordion qld__accordion--closed\" aria-controls=\"sunshine-coast-and-central-queensland-118323-345\" aria-expanded=\"false\" type=\"button\">\n  1012→                            Sunshine Coast and Central Queensland\n  1013→                        </button>\n  1014→            \n  1015→                        <div class=\"qld__accordion__body qld__accordion--closed\" id=\"sunshine-coast-and-central-queensland-118323-345\">\n  1016→                            <div class=\"qld__accordion__body-wrapper\">\n  1017→                                <p><strong>Central Queensland Indigenous Development</strong></p><p>Project: Deadly Futures &ndash; Ready for Work program</p><p>Deadly Futures is a 12-week employment readiness initiative for First Nations youth aged 13&ndash;17 years, including cultural mentorship and skills development activities to promote positive behaviour and a pathway to education, training, or employment.</p><p>Location: Bundaberg, Rockhampton, Woorabinda</p><p><strong>Lookout 07</strong></p><p>Project: The Youth Leadership Program</p><p>This program provides support for 12&ndash;17-year-olds through mentoring, mindset coaching, and job-readiness training over a period of 10 weeks.</p><p>Location: Sunshine Coast</p><p><strong>South Burnett CTC Incorporated</strong></p><p>Project: Safer Pathways</p><p>This initiative provides support over 15 months for disengaged, homeless, or at-risk youth aged 8-17 years, offering individualised support plans, structured peer group activities, emotional regulation and community re-engagement sessions to help get them back on track.</p><p>Location: South Burnett</p>\n  1018→                            </div>\n  1019→                        </div>\n  1020→                    </section>\n  1021→                </li>\n  1022→                <li>\n  1023→                    <section class=\"qld__accordion\">\n  1024→                        <button class=\"qld__accordion__title js-qld__accordion qld__accordion--closed\" aria-controls=\"north-queensland-118323-347\" aria-expanded=\"false\" type=\"button\">\n  1025→                            North Queensland\n  1026→                        </button>\n  1027→            \n  1028→                        <div class=\"qld__accordion__body qld__accordion--closed\" id=\"north-queensland-118323-347\">\n  1029→                            <div class=\"qld__accordion__body-wrapper\">\n  1030→                                <p><strong>Brodie Germaine Fitness Aboriginal Corporation </strong></p><p>Project: CAMPFIRE &ndash; Cultural Advancement and Mentoring Program</p><p>This 18-month program is led by Elders, cultural leaders, and trained mentors to strengthen cultural identity, emotional regulation, and positive relationships while re-engaging youth with education and employment.</p><p>Location: Bouila, Doomadgee, Mount Isa</p><p><strong>Family and Childrens Emerging Support Services </strong></p><p>Project: The Youth Leadership program</p><p>The Youth Leadership program provides support for 12&ndash;17-year-olds through cultural mentoring, mental health and housing support, as well as life skills education, including literacy, hygiene, and budgeting.</p><p>Location: Mackay</p><p><strong>NQ Ummah Care</strong></p><p>Project: Pathways to Engagement (PE) for Culturally Diverse Youth</p><p>This program provides 16 months&rsquo; of support to youth from migrant backgrounds, empowering at-risk youth to make positive life choices through soccer-based activities, life skill workshops and mentorship, preventing youth offending, and improving education and employment outcomes.</p><p>Location: Townsville</p><p><strong>Mudth-Niyleta Aboriginal and Torres Strait Islander Corporation </strong></p><p>Project: Youth Wellbeing</p><p>This program offers support to disengaged, homeless, or at-risk youth aged 8&ndash;17 years to re-engage with education, employment, and the community through case management care plans, referrals to allied health services, mentorship and networking opportunities.</p><p>Location: Mackay</p><p><strong>Silver Lining Foundation</strong></p><p>Project: Out of Hours Support program</p><p>Delivered by First Nations mentors, the Out of Hours Support program provides activity-based mentoring for 8&ndash;17-year-olds over 16 months, offering structured support during weekends, afternoons, and school holidays to reduce criminal behaviour by engaging youth in positive, culturally appropriate activities and fostering pro-social connections.</p><p>Location: Townsville</p><p><strong>Townsville Fire Limited </strong></p><p>Project: Pathways to Empowerment - Building Brighter Futures for at-risk youth</p><p>Participants will undertake a 10-week program, including weekly basketball training and mentoring sessions with Townsville Fire athletes. This program offers a range of supports to young people aged 10-17 years in the Townsville region, combining sport-based activities, mentoring, life skills workshops, and cultural interventions to re-engage at-risk youth back into education, the community, and future pathways.</p><p>Location: Townsville</p>\n  1031→                            </div>\n  1032→                        </div>\n  1033→                    </section>\n  1034→                </li>\n  1035→                <li>\n  1036→                    <section class=\"qld__accordion\">\n  1037→                        <button class=\"qld__accordion__title js-qld__accordion qld__accordion--closed\" aria-controls=\"far-north-queensland-118323-349\" aria-expanded=\"false\" type=\"button\">\n  1038→                            Far North Queensland\n  1039→                        </button>\n  1040→            \n  1041→                        <div class=\"qld__accordion__body qld__accordion--closed\" id=\"far-north-queensland-118323-349\">\n  1042→                            <div class=\"qld__accordion__body-wrapper\">\n  1043→                                <p><strong>Aspire Cairns Community Limited</strong></p><p>Project: Learn, Lead, Play and Thrive &ndash; Where Sport Fuels Success</p><p>A sport-for-development model that prioritises Aboriginal and Torres Strait Islander youth, girls, and underrepresented groups aged 8&ndash;17 years, focusing on physical activity, cultural connection, education support, and mentoring to build resilience, foster community connections, and improve outcomes.</p><p>Location: Cairns</p><p><strong>Australian Training Works Group Pty Ltd </strong></p><p>Project: The Rebuild Project</p><p>The Rebuild project supports youth aged 15-17 years to build skills and contribute to community through a structured program including daily mechanical training and free repair services for residents in need, fostering positive pathways, community connection, and a sense of purpose for participants.</p><p>Location: Cairns</p><p><strong>Bori Muy Limited</strong></p><p>Project: Connecting The Dots Youth Program</p><p>This is a 12-week initiative supports Aboriginal and Torres Strait Islander youth aged 8&ndash;17 yeas through one-on-one mentoring, culturally safe health workshops, and pro-social community activities, including&nbsp;&nbsp;&ldquo;On Country&rdquo; cultural camps.</p><p>Location: Cairns</p><p><strong>Desert Pea Association Inc</strong></p><p>Project: CROSSROADS &ndash; Kuranda</p><p>A 12-month program targeting at-risk Indigenous youth aged 12&ndash;17, using digital media and cultural frameworks to address anti-social behaviour and disconnection.</p><p>Location: Mareeba</p><p><strong>Jabalbina Yalanji Aboriginal Corporation </strong></p><p>Project: Jabalbina On Country Cultural Workshops</p><p>This workshop provides a 12-week program of cultural activities for at-risk 10&ndash;17-year-olds, including storytelling, bush skills, and artifact making.</p><p>Location: Cairns</p><p><strong>Prosocial Skills Development</strong></p><p>Project: Mastering Me</p><p>Master Me is a one year long early intervention program supporting youths aged 8&ndash;17 years with emerging antisocial behaviours by combining mentoring, activity-based learning, and prosocial skills development to foster emotional regulation, build relationships, and create a supportive therapeutic community.</p><p>Location: Cairns</p><p><strong>Thrive and Connect </strong></p><p>Project: Thrive Guiding</p><p>Thrive Guiding will support youth aged 10&ndash;14 years in the Cairns region over 13 months. With four 10-week intensive sessions, the program provides one-on-one mentoring and team building exercises to build cultural identity, belonging, and pathways to education, training, and community.</p><p>Location: Cairns</p>\n  1044→                            </div>\n  1045→                        </div>\n  1046→                    </section>\n  1047→                </li>\n  1048→ id=\"content\">\n   941→                        \n   942→                                <h1>Kickstarter program</h1>\n   943→                \n   944→                <!-- Page Contents Render -->\n   945→                \n   946→<data class=\"fb-component-track\" value=\"37602.page_alert\" data-name=\"page_alert\" data-date_created=\"2024-12-24 12:44:50\" data-date_updated=\"2026-03-11 09:32:45\" data-date_published=\"2026-03-11 09:32:45\"></data>\n   947→\n   948→<section class=\"qld__body qld__page-alerts--wrapper\" id=\"page-alert-37602\">\n   949→    <div class=\"container-fluid\">\n   950→        <div class=\"qld__page-alerts qld__page-alerts--info\">\n   951→                <div class=\"qld__page-alerts--heading qld__display-lg\">Kickstarter program update</div>\n   952→                <div><p>Grant applications for Rounds 1 and 2 of the Kickstarter program have concluded. Round 3 will be announced in 2026.</p></div>\n   953→        </div>\n   954→    </div>\n   955→</section>\n   956→\n   957→<p>The Queensland Government is following through with its commitment to restore safety where you live by delivering new, community-led early intervention programs to prevent youth crime</p><p>The Kickstarter program will trial the best, new initiatives for at-risk youth showing early signs of criminal behaviour and re-engage them with education, training and the community.</p><p><a href=\"#round-1-successful-applicants\">Find a local Kickstarter program</a></p><p>Across four years, a total of $50 million in funding will be committed to the program.</p><div><p>Grants of up to $300,000 (excl. GST) will be available to initiatives that focus on:</p><ul><li>reducing crime</li><li>re-engaging youth with education, training, or employment</li><li>boosting participation in the community</li><li>repairing relationships with family.</li></ul><p>Funded initiatives will address the underlining causes of disengagement, anti-social or criminal behaviour and provide youth with support, connections and guidance to get them back on track.</p></div><h2>Subscribe for updates</h2><p><a href=\"https://ems.gs/3Hyb0bXgysI\">Join our mailing list</a> to receive updates on the Kickstarter program and future Youth Justice and Victim Support funding opportunities.</p><h2>Who we are looking for</h2><p><strong>Grant applications for Rounds 1 and 2 have concluded. Round 3 will be announced in 2026.</strong></p><p>Kickstarter grants are for organisations that deliver community-led initiatives focused on reducing youth crime, boosting education, and providing training, or employment for at-risk youths.&nbsp;&nbsp;Applicants must show their program can effectively address these priorities.</p><p>An ideal proposal will include:</p><ul><li>a pro-social, activity-based engagement or concept for individuals and groups aged 8 to 17 years old<br />and be: <ul><li>targeted at prevention and early intervention responses</li><li>aimed at reducing youth crime and boosting education</li><li>provide training, and/or employment pathways for youths</li></ul></li><li>a response to local youth crime matters in your community, including how your idea/project aligns with community need</li><li>a demonstration of how your idea/project addresses anti-social behaviour and improves community safety</li><li>a performance and outcomes measure that reflects the needs and aspirations of youths in the community.</li></ul><p>Programs demonstrating measurable positive impact may be eligible for ongoing funding.</p><h2>Application process</h2><p>Kickstarter Round 3 grants will open in 2026.</p><p>To help you prepare, consider the following:</p><ol><li>Read the Round 2&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.publications.qld.gov.au/dataset/1fff06e2-0b11-4dfa-afaa-f23d55fc8f8a/resource/7f21ff89-1243-4eaa-9f47-4aba4e92d34d/download/kickstarter-grants-program-information-and-grant-guidelines.pdf\">Kickstarter program information and guidelines (PDF, 446KB)</a> to understand the eligibility and program funding guidelines. The final guidelines will be available when Round 3 grants open.</li><li>Read our <a href=\"https://www.youthjustice.qld.gov.au/partnerships/kickstarter-grants/how-to-prepare-your-application\">step-by-step guide</a>.</li><li>Consider how your proposal aligns with community needs, including: <ol><li>how your proposal specifically addresses the identified risks and needs of the youths in the community</li><li>how your idea/project will deliver a response, either directly or through referrals</li><li>evidence of how your proposal will reduce anti-social behaviour, youth crime, and improve community safety</li><li>who will be involved in the delivery of your response, and evidence of their commitment.</li></ol></li></ol><p>Round 3 grant applications must be completed and submitted online via the SmartyGrants website, which will open when Round 3 begins.</p><p>You will receive an acknowledgement email from SmartyGrants once you submit your application. If you don't receive an acknowledgement email, your application has not been submitted.</p><p>The SmartyGrants system will automatically shut off at midday on the closing dates of each round and will not allow applications to be submitted.</p><h2>Further information</h2><p>For further information, contact us at&nbsp;<a href=\"mailto:YJ_Grants@youthjustice.qld.gov.au\">YJ_Grants@youthjustice.qld.gov.au</a>.</p>\n   958→<data class=\"fb-component-track\" value=\"118323.accordion\" data-name=\"accordion\"
